</ul>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td class="hlist noprint nowrap" colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-top: 1px solid #aaa; padding-top: 3px;">\n         <a href="/wiki/Pacific_hurricane" title="Pacific hurricane">\n          Pacific hurricane seasons\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         <a href="/wiki/1992_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1992 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1992\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/1993_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1993 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1993\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <b>\n          1994\n         </b>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/1995_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1995 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1995\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/1996_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1996 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1996\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <b>\n        1994 Pacific hurricane season\n       </b>\n       was the final season of the eastern north Pacific\'s most recent active string of hurricane seasons that unofficially started in\n       <a href="/wiki/1981_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1981 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1981\n       </a>\n       . The season officially started on May 15, 1994, in the eastern Pacific, and on June 1, 1994, in the central Pacific, and lasted until November 30, 1994. These dates conventionally delimit the period of each year when most tropical cyclones form in the northeastern Pacific Ocean. The first\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       formed on June 18, while the last system dissipated on October 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This season, twenty-two tropical cyclones formed in the north Pacific Ocean east of the dateline, with all but two becoming tropical storms or hurricanes. A total of 10 hurricanes occurred, including five major hurricanes.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Of note in this season is an unusual spree of very intense storms. Hurricanes\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emilia_(1994)" title="Hurricane Emilia (1994)">\n        Emilia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilma_(1994)" title="Hurricane Gilma (1994)">\n        Gilma\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_John_(1994)" title="Hurricane John (1994)">\n        John\n       </a>\n       , and Olivia all reached a pressure below 930\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Millibars" title="Millibars">\n        millibars\n       </a>\n       . Longevity-wise, no tropical cyclone of any basin had previously persisted for as long as Hurricane John, which lasted 31 days. Elsewhere,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rosa_(1994)" title="Hurricane Rosa (1994)">\n        Hurricane Rosa\n       </a>\n       caused four casualties in Mexico as the basin\'s lone landfalling tropical storm or hurricane, and later was responsible for flooding in\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">\n        Texas\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Season_summary">\n        Season summary\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Season summary">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <center>\n       <div class="timeline-wrapper">\n        <map id="timeline_1b03a1d950be65b7686ea198be01f427" name="timeline_1b03a1d950be65b7686ea198be01f427">\n         <area alt="Hurricane John (1994)" coords="428,49,486,70" href="/wiki/Hurricane_John_(1994)"      <area alt="Hurricane Emilia (1994)" coords="233,62,302,83" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emilia_(1994)" shape="rect" title="Hurricane Emilia (1994)"/>\n         <area alt="Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale" coords="602,180,804,200" href="/wiki/Saffir%2DSimpson_Hurricane_Scale" shape="rect" title="Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale"/>\n        </map>\n        <img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/1b03a1d950be65b7686ea198be01f427.png" usemap="#timeline_1b03a1d950be65b7686ea198be01f427"/>\n       </div>\n      </center>\n      <table align="right" class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th colspan="3">\n         <b>\n          Most intense Pacific\n          <br/>\n          hurricane seasons\n         </b>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Rank\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Pacific_hurricane_seasons" title="List of Pacific hurricane seasons">\n          Season\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         <a href="/wiki/Accumulated_cyclone_energy" title="Accumulated cyclone energy">\n          ACE\n         </a>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         1\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1992_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1992 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1992\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         295\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         2\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2015 Pacific hurricane season">\n          2015\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         286\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         3\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1990_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1990 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1990\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         250\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         4\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1978_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1978 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1978\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         207\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         5\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1983_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1983 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1983\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         203\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         6\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1993_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1993 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1993\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         201\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         7\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/2014_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2014 Pacific hurricane season">\n          2014\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         198\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         8\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1984_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1984 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1984\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         193\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         9\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a href="/wiki/1985_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1985 Pacific hurricane season">\n          1985\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         192\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         10\n        </th>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         <a class="mw-selflink selflink">\n          1994\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:center;">\n         185\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       This season, twenty-two\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclones" title="Tropical cyclones">\n        tropical cyclones\n       </a>\n       formed in the north Pacific Ocean east of the dateline. All but two of them became tropical storms or hurricanes. In the Eastern Pacific region (\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140\xc2\xb0W\n       </a>\n       to North America), nineteen tropical depressions formed, of which seventeen became tropical storms, nine further intensifying into hurricanes, and five ultimately reaching major hurricanes of Category\xc2\xa03 intensity or higher on the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir-Simpson_Hurricane_Scale" title="Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale">\n        Saffir Simpson Scale\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These numbers are slightly above the long-term averages of fifteen tropical storms, nine hurricanes, and four major hurricanes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EPac_background_info_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EPac_background_info-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_Pacific_Hurricane_Center" title="Central Pacific Hurricane Center">\n        Central Pacific Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Area_of_responsibility" title="Area of responsibility">\n        area of responsibility\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140\xc2\xb0W\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">\n        International Date Line\n       </a>\n       ), three depressions, two tropical storms, and one hurricane formed. Overall, there were eleven tropical cyclones, eight tropical storms, five hurricanes, and three major hurricanes that formed or entered the Central Pacific region.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_main_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC_main-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These numbers are well above the long-term average of four tropical cyclones, two hurricanes, one tropical storm, and two depressions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC2006_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC2006-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The exceptionally high activity was contributed to by an\n       <a href="/wiki/El_Ni%C3%B1o" title="El Ni\xc3\xb1o">\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o\n       </a>\n       ongoing at the time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC1997_5-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC1997-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The only named storm to make landfall this year was\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rosa_(1994)" title="Hurricane Rosa (1994)">\n        Hurricane Rosa\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which killed four people in Western Mexico\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rosa2_6-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rosa2-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and forced over 400 to be evacuated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daily_Herald_7-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Daily_Herald-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other notable storms include Hurricane Olivia, a high-end Category 4 system,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the three Category\xc2\xa05 hurricanes\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emilia_(1994)" title="Hurricane Emilia (1994)">\n        Emilia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilma_(1994)" title="Hurricane Gilma (1994)">\n        Gilma\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_John_(1994)" title="Hurricane John (1994)">\n        John\n       </a>\n       . Both John and Hurricane Li existed in two of the three\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_basin" title="Tropical cyclone basin">\n        basins\n       </a>\n       (East, and West) of the Pacific Ocean.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       This season marked the end of the Northeastern Pacific\'s most recent active period, which began in\n       <a href="/wiki/1982_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1982 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1982\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Padgett_April_2004_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Padgett_April_2004-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and includes the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pacific_hurricanes#Highest" title="List of Pacific hurricanes">\n        five most active Pacific hurricane seasons\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Padgett_April_2004_9-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Padgett_April_2004-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Beginning in\n       <a href="/wiki/1995_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1995 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1995\n       </a>\n       , multi-decadal factors switched to a phase that suppresses Pacific hurricane activity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2008_Forecast_10-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2008_Forecast-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Since then, Pacific hurricane seasons have generally been below normal;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Historic_EPac_Seasonal_Activity_11-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Historic_EPac_Seasonal_Activity-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the lone abnormally active season since then was in\n       <a href="/wiki/1997_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1997 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1997\n       </a>\n       , where a strong El Nino event was observed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Padgett_April_2004_9-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Padgett_April_2004-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The 1994 Pacific hurricane season set several records. First, three hurricanes reached Category\xc2\xa05 intensity on the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir-Simpson_Hurricane_Scale" title="Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale">\n        Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       setting a record later tied in\n       <a href="/wiki/2002_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2002 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2002\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hurricane John lasted longer and spent more time tropical than any other tropical cyclone on Earth in recorded history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-e6_12-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-e6-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eleven tropical cyclones entered or formed in the central Pacific, a record shared with the\n       <a href="/wiki/1992_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1992 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1992 season\n       </a>\n       until\n       <a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2015 Pacific hurricane season">\n        the 2015 season\n       </a>\n       broke the record.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC1997_5-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC1997-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Finally, of the four most intense hurricanes recorded in the Central Pacific, three of them occurred this season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_main_3-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC_main-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The season began with the formation of Tropical Depression One-E on June 18 and ended with the dissipation of Tropical Depression Nona on October 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No named systems formed in May, three in June, four in July, five in August, six in September, two in October, and none in November.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The total length of the season, from the formation of the first depression to the dissipation of the last, was 130 days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EPAC_HURDAT_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EPAC_HURDAT-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table align="right" class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th align="center" colspan="6">\n         <b>\n          Accumulated Cyclone Energy\n         </b>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n   <td>\n         3.16\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emilia_(1994)" title="Hurricane Emilia (1994)">\n          Gilma\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         5.80 (18.8)\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         13\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Aletta\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1.42\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         4\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Olivia\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         16.5\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         14\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Miriam\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1.30\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         5\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Lane\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         12.7\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         15\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Paul\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1.22\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         6\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Carlotta\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         10.5\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         16\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Mele\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         (0.980)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         7\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a       <td>\n         Fabio\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.65\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         8\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Kristy\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1.02 (5.16)\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         18\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Norman\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.613\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         9\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Daniel\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2.91 (2.22)\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         19\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Bud\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.565\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         10\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Li\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         (4.48)\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         20\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Nona\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         (0.123)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th colspan="6">\n         Total: 78.0 (107)\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Accumulated_Cyclone_Energy" title="Accumulated Cyclone Energy">\n        Accumulated Cyclone Energy\n       </a>\n       (ACE) is a measure of how active a hurricane season is. It is calculated by squaring the windspeed of a cyclone with at least tropical storm-force winds every six hours, summing the results, and dividing that total by 10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       . As a tropical cyclone does not have gale-force winds until it becomes a tropical storm, tropical depressions are not included in these tables. For all storms, ACE is given to three\n       <a href="/wiki/Significant_figures" title="Significant figures">\n        significant figures\n       </a>\n       . The ACE in the east Pacific proper (\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140\xc2\xb0W\n       </a>\n       to North America) is given; the ACE in the central Pacific (the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">\n        International Date Line\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140\xc2\xb0W\n       </a>\n       ) is given in brackets. The table includes the ACE for Li and John only during those storm\'s time east of the dateline. Their ACE west of the dateline is part of the totals of the\n       <a href="/wiki/1994_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="1994 Pacific typhoon season">\n        1994 typhoon season\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       uses ACE to rank hurricane seasons as above-normal, near-normal, and below-normal. It defines below-normal as having an ACE less than 95*10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ; It defines above normal as having an ACE above 150*10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       along with the numbers of any two of the following above average: tropical storms (15), hurricanes (9), or major hurricanes (4); It defines near-normal as having an ACE between 100*10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       and 150*10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       , or an ACE above 150*10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       with fewer than two of the numbers of the following above average: tropical storms (15), hurricanes (9), or major hurricanes (4).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EPac_background_info_2-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EPac_background_info-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       This season has a total of seventeen tropical storms, nine hurricanes, and five major hurricanes. The total ACE of this season is 185*10\n       <sup>\n        4\n       </sup>\n       kt\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       . This qualifies this season as above-normal.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EPac_background_info_2-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EPac_background_info-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Systems">\n        Systems\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Systems">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Aletta">\n        Tropical Storm Aletta\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Aletta">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Aletta_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Aletta (1994).JPG" data-file-height="254" data-file-width="307" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Tropical_Storm_Aletta_%281994%29.JPG/150px-Tropical_Storm_Aletta_%281994%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Tropical_Storm_Aletta_%281994%29.JPG/225px-Tropical_Storm_Aletta_%281994%29.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Tropical_Storm_Aletta_%281994%29.JPG/300px-Tropical_Storm_Aletta_%281994%29.JPG 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aletta_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Aletta 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Aletta_1994_track.png/150px-Aletta_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Aletta_1994_track.png/225px-Aletta_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Aletta_1994_track.png/300px-Aletta_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         June 18\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 June 23\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         50\xc2\xa0mph (85\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         999\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Tropical Depression One-E formed from an area of disturbed weather on June 18. It strengthened to Tropical Storm Aletta the next day. It continued intensifying and reached its peak intensity on June 20. Vertical\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       began to weaken the storm thereafter. The weakening trend continued, weakening Aletta to a depression on June 21. The system dissipated June 23. Aletta\'s remnant low, however, could be tracked on satellite images for days following the storm. The low finally dissipated north of Hawaii.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Aletta1_14-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Aletta1-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Aletta never affected land, and no damage or casualties were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Aletta2_15-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Aletta2-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Bud">\n        Tropical Storm Bud\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Bud">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TropStormBud1994.JPG">\n            <img alt="TropStormBud1994.JPG" data-file-height="180" data-file-width="188" height="144" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/TropStormBud1994.JPG/150px-TropStormBud1994.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/29/TropStormBud1994.JPG 1.5x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bud_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Bud 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Bud_1994_track.png/150px-Bud_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Bud_1994_track.png/225px-Bud_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Bud_1994_track.png/300px-Bud_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         June 27\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 June 29\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1003\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Tropical Depression Two-E formed on June 27 about 575 miles (925\xc2\xa0km) south-southwest of the tip of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       . The depression headed west-northwest, gradually turned to the northwest, and strengthened into Tropical Storm Bud on June 27. Early the next day, Bud peaked in intensity.\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        Shear\n       </a>\n       caused by a nearby\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">\n        upper level low\n       </a>\n       slowly weakened Bud. Later on June 28, a second center of circulation developed. The two centers started a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fujiwhara_interaction" title="Fujiwhara interaction">\n        Fujiwhara interaction\n       </a>\n       . The second center then became dominant and the first one vanished. This confused structure is similar to what happened to\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Arlene_(1993)" title="Tropical Storm Arlene (1993)">\n        1993\'s Tropical Storm Arlene\n       </a>\n       . This confused structure also weakened Bud to a tropical depression on the afternoon of the same day the second center formed. Bud then headed westward over cool waters and dissipated on June 29.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bud1_16-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Bud1-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Tropical Storm Bud spent its entire life over the open ocean far from land areas. No casualties or damage was reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bud2_17-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Bud2-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Carlotta">\n        Hurricane Carlotta\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Hurricane Carlotta">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Carlotta_1994.JPG">\n            <img alt="Hurricane Carlotta 1994.JPG" data-file-height="212" data-file-width="285" height="112" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Hurricane_Carlotta_1994.JPG/150px-Hurricane_Carlotta_1994.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Hurricane_Carlotta_1994.JPG/225px-Hurricane_Carlotta_1994.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/08/Hurricane_Carlotta_1994.JPG 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Carlotta_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Carlotta 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Carlotta_1994_track.png/150px-Carlotta_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Carlotta_1994_track.png/225px-Carlotta_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Carlotta_1994_track.png/300px-Carlotta_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         June 28\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 5\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         967\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The tropical depression that would be Carlotta formed on June 28. It quickly became Tropical Storm Carlotta, and a large\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       became visible. Because of this, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        NHC\n       </a>\n       upgraded the storm to a hurricane. Carlotta peaked in intensity on July 1, as a 105\xc2\xa0mph (169\xc2\xa0km/h) hurricane. It gradually weakened as it moved into cooler waters, dissipating on July 5. Carlotta did not threaten land.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Carlotta1_18-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Carlotta1-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Carlotta buffeted\n       <a href="/wiki/Socorro_Island" title="Socorro Island">\n        Socorro Island\n       </a>\n       with sustained winds of 39\xc2\xa0mph (63\xc2\xa0km/h) on June 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Carlotta1_18-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Carlotta1-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Carlotta2_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Carlotta2-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other than there, Carlotta caused no damage or deaths.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Carlotta2_19-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Carlotta2-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Daniel">\n        Tropical Storm Daniel\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Daniel">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TropicalStormDaniel(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="TropicalStormDaniel(1994).JPG" data-file-height="260" data-file-width="343" height="114" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/TropicalStormDaniel%281994%29.JPG/150px-TropicalStormDaniel%281994%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/TropicalStormDaniel%281994%29.JPG/225px-TropicalStormDaniel%281994%29.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/TropicalStormDaniel%281994%29.JPG/300px-TropicalStormDaniel%281994%29.JPG 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Daniel_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Daniel 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Daniel_1994_track.png/150px-Daniel_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Daniel_1994_track.png/225px-Daniel_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Daniel_1994_track.png/300px-Daniel_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 8\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 14\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         65\xc2\xa0mph (100\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         993\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On July 8, a disturbance located about 1,000 miles (1,600\xc2\xa0km) southwest of the southern tip of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       developed a circulation and became Tropical Depression Four-E.\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_convection" title="Atmospheric convection">\n        Convection\n       </a>\n       increased, and the depression strengthened into Tropical Storm Daniel. Upper-level\n       <a href="/wiki/Outflow_(meteorology)" title="Outflow (meteorology)">\n        outflow\n       </a>\n       improved, and Daniel peaked in intensity on July 9. Daniel slowly declined as it continued westward. It entered the central Pacific on July 11.\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        Wind shear\n       </a>\n       weakened Daniel as it approached the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaii_(island)" title="Hawaii (island)">\n        Big Island\n       </a>\n       , and by July 15 had degenerated into an open wave.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daniel1_20-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Daniel1-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       When Daniel was approaching Hawaii, moderate surf of 4 to 6 feet (1.2 to 1.8\xc2\xa0m) impacted the south and southeast shores of the Big Island on July 13 and 14. Daniel\'s remnants also passed about 100 miles (160\xc2\xa0km) south of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Point,_Hawaii" title="South Point, Hawaii">\n        South Point, Hawaii\n       </a>\n       , on July 15. That day, they caused rainfall on windward slopes of the Big Island locally reaching 5 inches (130\xc2\xa0mm).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No reports of damage or casualties were received.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daniel2_21-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Daniel2-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Emilia">\n        Hurricane Emilia\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Hurricane Emilia">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff6060">\n         Category 5\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Hurricane Emilia 19 july 1994 1656Z.jpg" data-file-height="760" data-file-width="760" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg/150px-Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg/225px-Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg/300px-Hurricane_Emilia_19_july_1994_1656Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Emilia_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Emilia 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Emilia_1994_track.png/150px-Emilia_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Emilia_1994_track.png/225px-Emilia_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Emilia_1994_track.png/300px-Emilia_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 16\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 25\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         160\xc2\xa0mph (260\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         926\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emilia_(1994)" title="Hurricane Emilia (1994)">\n        Hurricane Emilia (1994)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On July 16, an\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">\n        area of low pressure\n       </a>\n       associated with a tropical wave organized into Tropical Depression Five-E. It strengthened into Tropical Storm Emilia later that day. It moved west-northwest and strengthened into a hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Emilia1_22-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Emilia1-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It entered the central Pacific on July 17. It continued intensifying, reaching Category\xc2\xa05 intensity on July 19,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the first Category\xc2\xa05 Pacific hurricane since\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ava_(1973)" title="Hurricane Ava (1973)">\n        Ava\n       </a>\n       . Emilia started weakening quickly on July 21. It weakened to a tropical storm on July 23 and dissipated two days later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Emilia passed south of the Hawaiian Islands, producing swells of 6 to 10 feet (1.8 to 3.0\xc2\xa0m) in height near the\n       <a href="/wiki/Puna,_Hawaii" title="Puna, Hawaii">\n        Puna\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ka%E2%80%98%C5%AB,_Hawaii" title="Ka\xe2\x80\x98\xc5\xab, Hawaii">\n        Ka\xe2\x80\x98\xc5\xab\n       </a>\n       coasts. Winds caused minor damage, and rain was moderate.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No one was killed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Emilia2_23-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Emilia2-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Fabio">\n        Tropical Storm Fabio\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Fabio">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TropStormFabio_1994.JPG">\n            <img alt="TropStormFabio 1994.JPG" data-file-height="260" data-file-width="273" height="143" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fabio_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Fabio 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Fabio_1994_track.png/150px-Fabio_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Fabio_1994_track.png/225px-Fabio_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Fabio_1994_track.png/300px-Fabio_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 19\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 24\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1002\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical depression formed on July 19. Later that day, it strengthened into Tropical Storm Fabio. Fabio headed generally west or northwestward.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fabio1_24-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Fabio1-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It entered the central Pacific as a tropical depression, and dissipated on July 24.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Fabio\'s remnants brought locally heavy rainfall to Hawaii, reaching 3 to 4 inches (76 to 102\xc2\xa0mm).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No one was killed and there was no damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fabio2_25-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Fabio2-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Gilma">\n        Hurricane Gilma\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Hurricane Gilma">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilma_(1994)" title="Hurricane Gilma (1994)">\n        Hurricane Gilma (1994)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff6060">\n         Category 5\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png">\n            <img alt="Gilma Jul 24 1994 0442Z.png" data-file-height="601" data-file-width="570" height="158" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png/150px-Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png/225px-Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png/300px-Gilma_Jul_24_1994_0442Z.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gilma_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Gilma 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Gilma_1994_track.png/150px-Gilma_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Gilma_1994_track.png/225px-Gilma_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Gilma_1994_track.png/300px-Gilma_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 21\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 July 31\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         160\xc2\xa0mph (260\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         920\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Part of a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       organized into a tropical depression on July 21. It headed westward and out to sea, strengthening into a tropical storm the next day. Gilma rapidly strengthened and became a hurricane exactly one day after it was named. It continued to intensify as it entered the central Pacific. Shortly after entering the central Pacific, Gilma reached Category\xc2\xa05 intensity on the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir-Simpson_Hurricane_Scale" title="Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale">\n        Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale\n       </a>\n       , the second of the season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gilma1_26-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Gilma1-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It then suddenly weakened for unexplained reasons, and weakened into a tropical storm on July 27. It became a depression three days after that and dissipated on July 31.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hurricane Gilma had minor impact on\n       <a href="/wiki/Johnston_Atoll" title="Johnston Atoll">\n        Johnston Atoll\n       </a>\n       . That atoll received light rain, wind gusts to near\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gale_force" title="Gale force">\n        gale force\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gilma2_27-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Gilma2-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and surf.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No casualties or damage were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gilma2_27-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Gilma2-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Gilma was the second most-intense Pacific at the time. As of 2016, it remains the ninth-most intense. Gilma is also the strongest July storm in the eastern or central Pacific.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Li">\n        Hurricane Li\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Hurricane Li">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Li_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Hurricane Li (1994).JPG" data-file-height="145" data-file-width="129" height="169" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Hurricane_Li_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Li_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Li 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Li_1994_track.png/150px-Li_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Li_1994_track.png/225px-Li_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Li_1994_track.png/300px-Li_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         July 31\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 12 (\n         <a href="/wiki/1994_Pacific_typhoon_season#Tropical_Storm_Li" title="1994 Pacific typhoon season">\n          Exited basin\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         75\xc2\xa0mph (120\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         \xe2\x89\xa4 1007\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical disturbance southwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cabo_San_Lucas" title="Cabo San Lucas">\n        Cabo San Lucas\n       </a>\n       organized into Tropical Depression Eight-E on July 31.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8EDiscussion1_28-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8EDiscussion1-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It headed west-northwest without strengthening much, and crossed into the central Pacific on August 2.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8eDiscussion10_29-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8eDiscussion10-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eight-E developed a second center of circulation, which became dominant,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8EDiscussion13_30-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8EDiscussion13-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and then became bound up in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intertropical_convergence_zone" title="Intertropical convergence zone">\n        intertropical convergence zone\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8EDiscussion16_31-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8EDiscussion16-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eight-E then became disorganized, with multiple centers of circulation,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8EDiscussion18_32-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8EDiscussion18-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and advisories were discontinued on August 5. The depression\'s remains continued their westward path well south of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaiian_Islands" title="Hawaiian Islands">\n        Hawaiian Islands\n       </a>\n       . The depression regenerated on August 8. It soon strengthened into a tropical storm and was named Li,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which is\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaiian_language" title="Hawaiian language">\n        Hawaiian\n       </a>\n       for "\n       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Lee" title="wikt:Lee">\n        Lee\n       </a>\n       ".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Li_etymology_33-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Li_etymology-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Li approached the dateline on its generally westward heading. Just before crossing, it intensified into a minimal Category\xc2\xa01 hurricane. It crossed the dateline on August 12 and became a storm in the\n       <a href="/wiki/1994_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="1994 Pacific typhoon season">\n        1994 Pacific typhoon season\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Wind shear from a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_upper-tropospheric_trough" title="Tropical upper-tropospheric trough">\n        tropical upper-tropospheric trough\n       </a>\n       weakened back into a tropical storm as it crossed the dateline, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">\n        Joint Typhoon Warning Center\n       </a>\n       downgraded Li with its first advisory.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JTWC_Li_106_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JTWC_Li_106-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Li stayed a tropical storm until August 16, where it weakened into a tropical depression. The system then began recurving, and dissipated on August 18.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JTWC_Li_105_35-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JTWC_Li_105-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A weakening Tropical Depression Li caused showers on\n       <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">\n        Wake Island\n       </a>\n       . Other than there, Li had no impact on any land, and no casualties or damage were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Li is one of only seven tropical cyclones to exist on all three\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_basin" title="Tropical cyclone basin">\n        tropical cyclone basins\n       </a>\n       in the Pacific Ocean. It is also one of only six systems to form as a depression in the east Pacific but be named in the central; the others are\n       <a href="/wiki/1984_Pacific_hurricane_season#Tropical_Storm_Lala" title="1984 Pacific hurricane season">\n        Lala\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Iniki" title="Hurricane Iniki">\n        Iniki\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/2009_Pacific_hurricane_season#Tropical_Storm_Lana" title="2009 Pacific hurricane season">\n        Lana\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_hurricane_season#Tropical_Storm_Ela" title="2015 Pacific hurricane season">\n        Ela\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/2016_Pacific_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Ulika" title="2016 Pacific hurricane season">\n        Ulika\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Hector">\n        Tropical Storm Hector\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Hector">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Hector_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Hector (1994).JPG" data-file-height="174" data-file-width="152" height="172" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Tropical_Storm_Hector_%281994%29.JPG/150px-Tropical_Storm_Hector_%281994%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/57/Tropical_Storm_Hector_%281994%29.JPG 1.5x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hector_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Hector 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Hector_1994_track.png/150px-Hector_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Hector_1994_track.png/225px-Hector_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Hector_1994_track.png/300px-Hector_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 7\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 10\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         65\xc2\xa0mph (100\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         993\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On August 7, a tropical depression formed from a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       a few hundred miles south of Baja California. It became Tropical Storm Hector quickly, and as it paralleled the coast of Mexico, it began to weaken, dissipating on August 10. No damage was reported anywhere.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hector1_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hector1-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Tropical Storm Hector was forecast to approach the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       . A\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_watches_and_warnings" title="Tropical cyclone watches and warnings">\n        tropical storm watch\n       </a>\n       was issued for part of the peninsula on August 8. It was lifted later the same day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hector2_37-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hector2-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hector\'s most significant impact was rain. The tropical storm dumped rain along a discontinuous zone of coastal and inland Mexico. The highest point maxima were 7.87 inches (200\xc2\xa0mm) at Cerro de Ortega/Ixtlahua and 7.60 inches (193\xc2\xa0mm) at Caduano/Santiago.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HPC_Hector_38-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HPC_Hector-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No damage or casualties were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hector2_37-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hector2-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_One-C">\n        Tropical Depression One-C\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression One-C">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TD_01C_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="TD 01C (1994).JPG" data-file-height="118" data-file-width="109" height="162" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/77/TD_01C_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:One-C_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="One-C 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/One-C_1994_track.png/150px-One-C_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/One-C_1994_track.png/225px-One-C_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/One-C_1994_track.png/300px-One-C_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 9\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 14\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         35\xc2\xa0mph (55\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       An area of disturbed weather organized into a tropical depression on August 9 while located 740 miles (1,190\xc2\xa0km) southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hilo,_Hawaii" title="Hilo, Hawaii">\n        Hilo, Hawaii\n       </a>\n       . The depression moved westward without organizing, and dissipated on August 14.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Moisture from the system produced heavy rainfall over the island of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaii_(island)" title="Hawaii (island)">\n        Hawaii\n       </a>\n       , totaling to over 15 inches (380\xc2\xa0mm).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The flooding closed all major roads in\n       <a href="/wiki/Hilo,_Hawaii" title="Hilo, Hawaii">\n        Hilo\n       </a>\n       , and was considered the worst flooding in 40\xc2\xa0years. The rainfall destroyed two homes and damaged 214, 14 severely. It also damaged roads and businesses. Damage throughout the island totaled to $5\xc2\xa0million (1994\xc2\xa0USD; $8.08\xc2\xa0million 2017\xc2\xa0USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NCDC1_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NCDC1-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding occurred in\n       <a href="/wiki/Maui" title="Maui">\n        Maui\n       </a>\n       as well, where landslides blocked portions of the Hana Highway.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NCDC2_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NCDC2-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One-C\'s point maximum of 15\xc2\xa0in (380\xc2\xa0mm) makes it Hawaii\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_wettest_tropical_cyclones_in_the_United_States#Hawaii" title="List of wettest tropical cyclones in the United States">\n        seventh wettest\n       </a>\n       known tropical cyclone.\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Ileana">\n        Hurricane Ileana\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Hurricane Ileana">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Ileana_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Hurricane Ileana (1994).JPG" data-file-height="158" data-file-width="158" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Hurricane_Ileana_%281994%29.JPG/150px-Hurricane_Ileana_%281994%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/bb/Hurricane_Ileana_%281994%29.JPG 1.5x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ileana_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Ileana 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Ileana_1994_track.png/150px-Ileana_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Ileana_1994_track.png/225px-Ileana_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Ileana_1994_track.png/300px-Ileana_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 10\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 14\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         75\xc2\xa0mph (120\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         986\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A disturbance that was part of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intertropical_convergence_zone" title="Intertropical convergence zone">\n        intertropical convergence zone\n       </a>\n       developed several centers of circulation. After it organized, it separated from the ITCZ and became Tropical Depression Eleven-E on August 10 while the system was about 690 miles (1,110\xc2\xa0km) south-southeast of the southern tip of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ileana1_41-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ileana1-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was upgraded to Tropical Storm Ileana at the second advisory,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IleanaDiscussion2_42-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-IleanaDiscussion2-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       at the same time as John, the next storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JohnDiscussion3_43-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JohnDiscussion3-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       appeared, and Ileana became a hurricane on August 12. It began weakening almost immediately thereafter, as it passed over cooler waters and encountered increasing wind shear. Ileana was a tropical storm on August 13, and the next day it was a dissipating swirl low-level clouds located about 520 miles (840\xc2\xa0km) west of\n       <a href="/wiki/Punta_Eugenia" title="Punta Eugenia">\n        Punta Eugenia\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ileana1_41-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ileana1-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although Ileana paralleled the coast of Mexico,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_watches_and_warnings" title="Tropical cyclone watches and warnings">\n        watches and warnings\n       </a>\n       were not issued because winds of tropical storm-force were not expected to affect land. No one was killed and there was no damage reported in association with this cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ileana2_44-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ileana2-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_John">\n        Hurricane John\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Hurricane John">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff6060">\n         Category 5\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Hurricane John 23 aug 1994 1739Z.jpg" data-file-height="608" data-file-width="540" height="169" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg/150px-Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg/225px-Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg/300px-Hurricane_John_23_aug_1994_1739Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:John_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="John 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/John_1994_track.png/150px-John_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/John_1994_track.png/225px-John_1994_track.png 1.5x,
