//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/John_1994_track.png/300px-John_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 11\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 10\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         175\xc2\xa0mph (280\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         929\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_John_(1994)" title="Hurricane John (1994)">\n        Hurricane John (1994)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Tropical Depression Ten-E formed on August 11 south of Mexico. It headed generally westward, and was upgraded into a tropical storm twelve hours after it formed and was named John. John fluctuated in strength as it headed west, always managing to stay at tropical storm strength. On August 20, steady intensification began, and John was a major hurricane when it entered the central Pacific. It continued westward, reaching Category\xc2\xa05 intensity on August 23. It passed around 245 miles (394\xc2\xa0km) south of Hawaii, and passed just north of Johnston Atoll on August 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-John1_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-John1-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       John stayed at hurricane intensity until it crossed the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">\n        dateline\n       </a>\n       on August 28, becoming a typhoon of the\n       <a href="/wiki/1994_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="1994 Pacific typhoon season">\n        1994 Pacific typhoon season\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After weakening into a tropical storm, John recurved, looped, and recurved again.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JTWCJohn_46-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JTWCJohn-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It reintensified, and was a hurricane when it recrossed the dateline to reenter the central Pacific. John headed north-northeast until it went extratropical on September 10,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       thirty one days after it formed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ahead of the hurricane, the 1100 people at\n       <a href="/wiki/Johnston_Atoll" title="Johnston Atoll">\n        Johnston Atoll\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Emergency_evacuation" title="Emergency evacuation">\n        evacuated\n       </a>\n       . On the atoll, John caused $15\xc2\xa0million (1994\xc2\xa0USD; $24.2\xc2\xa0million 2017\xc2\xa0USD) in damage. No deaths were reported. Other than on Johnston, Hurricane John had minor effects in Hawaii. Its remnants also affected Alaska.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane John was the longest lasting and farthest traveling tropical cyclone on Earth in recorded history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-e6_12-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-e6-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It is also one of six tropical cyclones to exist in all three\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_basins" title="Tropical cyclone basins">\n        basins\n       </a>\n       of the Pacific Ocean, an uncommon west-to-east dateline crosser, and one of the few tropical cyclone to cross the dateline more than once.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Twelve-E">\n        Tropical Depression Twelve-E\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression Twelve-E">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TD_12E_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="TD 12E (1994).JPG" data-file-height="147" data-file-width="142" height="155" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f0/TD_12E_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Twelve-E_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Twelve-E 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Twelve-E_1994_track.png/150px-Twelve-E_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Twelve-E_1994_track.png/225px-Twelve-E_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Twelve-E_1994_track.png/300px-Twelve-E_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 12\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 15\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         35\xc2\xa0mph (55\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1006\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On August 14, an area of convection organized enough to be considered a tropical depression. It was steered by John\'s circulation, and it was never expected to strengthen much because it was close to cool waters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12E1_47-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12E1-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone drifted north, then northeast, north again, northwest, and then west.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12E_report_48-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12E_report-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       declared the depression dissipated on August 15.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12E5_49-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12E5-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The depression had no effects anywhere.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12E_report_48-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12E_report-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Kristy">\n        Hurricane Kristy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Hurricane Kristy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Kristy_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Hurricane Kristy (1994).JPG" data-file-height="123" data-file-width="122" height="151" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/24/Hurricane_Kristy_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kristy_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Kristy 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Kristy_1994_track.png/150px-Kristy_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Kristy_1994_track.png/225px-Kristy_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Kristy_1994_track.png/300px-Kristy_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 28\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 5\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         \xe2\x89\xa4 992\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On August 28, Tropical Depression Thirteen-E formed about 1,300 miles (2,100\xc2\xa0km) southwest of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cabo_San_Lucas,_Mexico" title="Cabo San Lucas, Mexico">\n        Cabo San Lucas, Mexico\n       </a>\n       . It was named Tropical Storm Kristy on August 30. As it crossed into the central Pacific, a banding-type\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       formed and it became a hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kristy1_50-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Kristy1-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Twelve hours later, it reached Category\xc2\xa02 intensity. Kristy weakened steadily from that point due to\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       . It passed about 300 miles (480\xc2\xa0km) south of Hawaii, and dissipated on September 5.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The lowest central pressure of Kristy is unknown. The last estimate was made when Kirsty was still a tropical storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As it approached the Hawaiian Islands, a high surf advisory and a high wind\n       <a href="/wiki/Severe_weather_terminology_(United_States)" title="Severe weather terminology (United States)">\n        warning\n       </a>\n       were issued for the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Big_Island_of_Hawaii" title="Big Island of Hawaii">\n        Big Island of Hawaii\n       </a>\n       . No damage or deaths were reported in association with this system.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kristy2_51-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Kristy2-51">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Its remnants crossed\n       <a href="/wiki/180th_meridian" title="180th meridian">\n        180th meridian\n       </a>\n       very early on September 7 and was absorbed by a tropical depression which became Typhoon Melissa in the\n       <a href="/wiki/1994_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="1994 Pacific typhoon season">\n        Western Pacific basin\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Lane">\n        Hurricane Lane\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Hurricane Lane">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Lane_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Hurricane Lane (1994).JPG" data-file-height="136" data-file-width="121" height="169" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c2/Hurricane_Lane_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lane_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Lane 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lane_1994_track.png/150px-Lane_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lane_1994_track.png/225px-Lane_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lane_1994_track.png/300px-Lane_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 3\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 10\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         948\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The same tropical wave that spawned\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_storms_in_the_1994_Atlantic_hurricane_season#Tropical_Depression_Five" title="List of storms in the 1994 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        Tropical Depression Five\n       </a>\n       in the Atlantic became Tropical Depression Fourteen-E on September 3. It quickly became Tropical Storm Lane. A high pressure ridge centered itself north of Lane, keeping the storm on a westward track. This brought Lane into very favorable conditions, and Lane intensified. When the tropical storm reached hurricane strength, it entered a phase of rapid intensification, reaching winds of about 135\xc2\xa0mph (217\xc2\xa0km/h), making it a category four hurricane. The high pressure ridge shifted eastward, and allowed Lane to enter unfavorable conditions. Lane dissipated on September 10.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Mele">\n        Tropical Storm Mele\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Mele">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Mele_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Mele (1994).JPG" data-file-height="107" data-file-width="103" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/15/Tropical_Storm_Mele_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mele_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Mele 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Mele_1994_track.png/150px-Mele_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Mele_1994_track.png/225px-Mele_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Mele_1994_track.png/300px-Mele_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 6\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 9\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         40\xc2\xa0mph (65\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical disturbance became Tropical Depression Two-C on September 6. It reached tropical storm strength the next day, being named Mele.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The name Mele means "\n       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/song" title="wikt:song">\n        song\n       </a>\n       " in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaiian_language" title="Hawaiian language">\n        Hawaiian language\n       </a>\n       and is also the Hawaiian form of "\n       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Mary" title="wikt:Mary">\n        Mary\n       </a>\n       ".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mele_etymology_53-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mele_etymology-53">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mele headed west-northwest and weakened back into a tropical depression on September. It dissipated later that day without incident.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Miriam">\n        Tropical Storm Miriam\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Miriam">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Miriam_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Miriam (1994).JPG" data-file-height="137" data-file-width="132" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Tropical_Storm_Miriam_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Miriam_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Miriam 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Miriam_1994_track.png/150px-Miriam_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Miriam_1994_track.png/225px-Miriam_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Miriam_1994_track.png/300px-Miriam_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 15\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 21\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1002\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Miriam formed from a weak disturbance on September 15. It strengthened slightly into Tropical Storm Miriam, and dissipated on September 21, having led an uneventful life without impact. In an interesting occurrence, the low-level remnants of Miriam were still visible for weeks after the storm dissipated near\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140\xc2\xb0W\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Miriam_54-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Miriam-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Norman">\n        Tropical Storm Norman\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Norman">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Norman_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Norman (1994).JPG" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="137" height="140" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/82/Tropical_Storm_Norman_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Norman_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Norman 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Norman_1994_track.png/150px-Norman_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Norman_1994_track.png/225px-Norman_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Norman_1994_track.png/300px-Norman_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 19\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 22\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         40\xc2\xa0mph (65\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1004\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical depression formed on September 19, and became Tropical Storm Norman the next day. After tracking northwest, it began to turn north in response to a trough, and convection began to diminish. Norman dissipated on September 22 without having ever affected land.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norman_55-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Norman-55">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Olivia">\n        Hurricane Olivia\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Hurricane Olivia">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Olivia_94_peak.jpg">\n            <img alt="Olivia 94 peak.jpg" data-file-height="380" data-file-width="380" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Olivia_94_peak.jpg/150px-Olivia_94_peak.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Olivia_94_peak.jpg/225px-Olivia_94_peak.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Olivia_94_peak.jpg/300px-Olivia_94_peak.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Olivia_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Olivia 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Olivia_1994_track.png/150px-Olivia_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Olivia_1994_track.png/225px-Olivia_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Olivia_1994_track.png/300px-Olivia_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 22\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 29\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         150\xc2\xa0mph (240\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         923\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Olivia ultimately formed from a disturbance that had separated from the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intertropical_convergence_zone" title="Intertropical convergence zone">\n        intertropical convergence zone\n       </a>\n       and become distinct by September 19. The disturbance slowly headed westward and it organized into a tropical depression on September 22 while located about 720 miles (1,160\xc2\xa0km) south of the southern tip of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       . The depression headed west-northwestwards and strengthened into Tropical Storm Olivia on September 22. It steadily intensified and was a hurricane on September 24. It then rapidly strengthened into a powerful major hurricane. It slowly curled to the northwest as it was\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_observation" title="Tropical cyclone observation">\n        observed\n       </a>\n       by NOAA research aircraft.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Olivia1_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Olivia1-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Olivia peaked in intensity on September 25. Meanwhile, a large\n       <a href="/wiki/Cyclone" title="Cyclone">\n        cyclone\n       </a>\n       off the extreme\n       <a href="/wiki/Southern_California" title="Southern California">\n        southern part of\n       </a>\n       California induced a northward path. As Olivia started a small anticyclonic loop,\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       began to weaken the hurricane. When Olivia was finished the loop, it had weakened to a tropical storm. It then headed westward. It weakened into a tropical depression on September 28 and dissipated the next day. No impact was reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Olivia2_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Olivia2-57">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       At the time, Olivia was the third-most intense Pacific hurricane on record. It has since dropped to eleventh. The storm also had the lowest\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_pressure" title="Atmospheric pressure">\n        barometric pressure\n       </a>\n       of a\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Category_4_Pacific_hurricanes" title="List of Category 4 Pacific hurricanes">\n        Category 4 Pacific hurricane\n       </a>\n       on record. In\n       <a href="/wiki/2001_Pacific_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Juliette" title="2001 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2001\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Juliette" title="Hurricane Juliette">\n        Hurricane Juliette\n       </a>\n       joined Olivia as the most intense Cat. 4 on record. In\n       <a href="/wiki/2014_Pacific_hurricane_season#Hurricane_Odile" title="2014 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2014\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Odile" title="Hurricane Odile">\n        Hurricane Odile\n       </a>\n       beat both storms when it attained a minimum pressure of 918\xc2\xa0mbars. Olivia was also the most intense September hurricane. Since,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Linda" title="Hurricane Linda">\n        Hurricane Linda\n       </a>\n       beat Olivia. Olivia remains the third most intense September hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Paul">\n        Tropical Storm Paul\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Paul">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Paul_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Paul (1994).JPG" data-file-height="139" data-file-width="135" height="154" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/92/Tropical_Storm_Paul_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Paul_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Paul 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Paul_1994_track.png/150px-Paul_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Paul_1994_track.png/225px-Paul_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Paul_1994_track.png/300px-Paul_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 24\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 30\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1003\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A nearly stationary cluster of thunderstorms and\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_convection" title="Atmospheric convection">\n        convection\n       </a>\n       that had been hanging around since September 15 and escaped destruction by Tropical Storm Miriam organized into Tropical Depression Eighteen-E on September 24. It was located between Miriam\'s remnants and the developing Olivia. It became Tropical Storm Paul on the afternoon of September 25. It peaked in intensity on September 27. Then, upper\n       <a href="/wiki/Outflow_(meteorology)" title="Outflow (meteorology)">\n        outflow\n       </a>\n       from the nearby Olivia started shearing the tropical cyclone. Paul had been completely destroyed by September 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paul1_58-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Paul1-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The tropical cyclone never threatened land, and consequently, no damage or deaths were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paul2_59-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Paul2-59">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Rosa">\n        Hurricane Rosa\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Hurricane Rosa">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rosa_(1994)" title="Hurricane Rosa (1994)">\n        Hurricane Rosa (1994)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Rosa oct 13 1994 1800Z.jpg" data-file-height="301" data-file-width="301" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg/150px-Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg/225px-Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg/300px-Rosa_oct_13_1994_1800Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Rosa_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Rosa 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Rosa_1994_track.png/150px-Rosa_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Rosa_1994_track.png/225px-Rosa_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Rosa_1994_track.png/300px-Rosa_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 8\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 15\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         974\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       An area of disturbed weather organized into a tropical depression at midday on October 8. It had trouble organizing, and advisories were discontinued for a while. The cyclone finally became a tropical storm on October 11 and was named Rosa. It moved glacially, but eventually a\n       <a href="/wiki/Trough_(meteorology)" title="Trough (meteorology)">\n        trough\n       </a>\n       steered Rosa north and then northeast. Rosa intensified quickly, peaking at Category\xc2\xa02 intensity just before landfall near\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=La_Concepci%C3%B3n,_Veracruz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="La Concepci\xc3\xb3n, Veracruz (page does not exist)">\n        La Concepci\xc3\xb3n\n       </a>\n       on the morning of October 14. Rosa quickly decayed over the mountains of Mexico, and its cloud shield rapidly accelerated northward through the United States, spreading moisture.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rosa1_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rosa1-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 12, a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        hurricane watch\n       </a>\n       was issued for the coast from\n       <a href="/wiki/Culiac%C3%A1n" title="Culiac\xc3\xa1n">\n        Culiac\xc3\xa1n\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Manzanillo,_Colima" title="Manzanillo, Colima">\n        Manzanillo\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baja_California_Peninsula" title="Baja California Peninsula">\n        Baja California Peninsula\n       </a>\n       south of\n       <a href="/wiki/24th_parallel_north" title="24th parallel north">\n        latitude 24\xc2\xb0N\n       </a>\n       . At the same time, a tropical storm warning was issued from Manzanillo to\n       <a href="/wiki/Tepic" title="Tepic">\n        Tepic\n       </a>\n       . On October 14, a hurricane warning was issued for the coast between Culiac\xc3\xa1n and\n       <a href="/wiki/Cabo_Corrientes,_Jalisco" title="Cabo Corrientes, Jalisco">\n        Cabo Corrientes, Jalisco\n       </a>\n       , and a tropical storm warning south of Cabo Corrientes to Manzanillo. All watches and warnings were lifted later that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rosa5_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rosa5-61">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Four deaths, two in each of\n       <a href="/wiki/Nayarit" title="Nayarit">\n        Nayarit\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Durango" title="Durango">\n        Durango\n       </a>\n       , were reported. Four people were missing in\n       <a href="/wiki/Sinaloa" title="Sinaloa">\n        Sinaloa\n       </a>\n       . All of the deaths were due to\n       <a href="/wiki/Drowning" title="Drowning">\n        drowning\n       </a>\n       . More than 100,000\xc2\xa0people had their homes damaged in Nayarit.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Telephone_pole" title="Telephone pole">\n        Telephone poles\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Electric_power_transmission" title="Electric power transmission">\n        power lines\n       </a>\n       were downed in Sinaloa. Rain caused\n       <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">\n        landslides\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Flash_flood" title="Flash flood">\n        flash-flooding\n       </a>\n       in mountainous areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rosa2_6-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rosa2-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Jalisco" title="Jalisco">\n        Jalisco\n       </a>\n       , mudslides forced the evacuation of 400 people from two coastal villages.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The highest rainfall total in Mexico was 14.09 inches (358\xc2\xa0mm) at Mesa de Pedro Pablo.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HPCRosa_63-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HPCRosa-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The moisture Rosa sent into the United States was a contributing factor in record rains in parts of southeastern Texas from October 15 to 19. Those rains caused flooding that killed 22 people, destroyed over 3000 homes, and caused US$700\xc2\xa0million in damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USGS_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-USGS-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Nona">\n        Tropical Storm Nona\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Nona">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tropical_Storm_Nona_(1994).JPG">\n            <img alt="Tropical Storm Nona (1994).JPG" data-file-height="186" data-file-width="150" height="186" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/66/Tropical_Storm_Nona_%281994%29.JPG" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nona_1994_track.png">\n            <img alt="Nona 1994 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Nona_1994_track.png/150px-Nona_1994_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Nona_1994_track.png/225px-Nona_1994_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Nona_1994_track.png/300px-Nona_1994_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 21\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 26\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         40\xc2\xa0mph (65\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Tropical Depression Three-C formed on October 21 in the Central Pacific basin. It traveled westward for about 4\xc2\xa0days before strengthening to Tropical Storm Nona on October 25.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The name "Nona" is\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaiian_language" title="Hawaiian language">\n        Hawaiian\n       </a>\n       for the Latin name spelled the\n       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Nona" title="wikt:Nona">\n        same way\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HawaiianClub_65-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HawaiianClub-65">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NonaEtymology_66-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NonaEtymology-66">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nona immediately weakened back into a tropical depression. Upper-level westerlies from a nearby\n       <a href="/wiki/Trough_(meteorology)" title="Trough (meteorology)">\n        trough\n       </a>\n       destroyed the depression on October 26. No deaths or damage were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPHC_8-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPHC-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nona was a tropical storm for six hours,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-best_track_1-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-best_track-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the minimum possible time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HURDAT_format_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HURDAT_format-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_storms">\n        Other storms\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Other storms">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Yuri">\n        Tropical Depression Yuri\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2"      <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 21\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 22 (\n         <a <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         30\xc2\xa0mph (45\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1004\n         <a </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       According to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">\n        Joint Typhoon Warning Center\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">\n        Japan Meteorological Agency\n       </a>\n       , on October\xc2\xa021 a tropical depression formed west of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Dateline" title="International Dateline">\n        International Dateline\n       </a>\n       , and soon it exited CPHC\'s area of responsibility;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMA_BT_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JMA_BT-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JTWC_BT_69-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JTWC_BT-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       however, this storm wasn\'t included into CPHC database. As it entered into western Pacific, it strengthened as a tropical storm and received the name\n       <i>\n        Yuri\n       </i>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Storm_names">\n        Storm names\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Storm names">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The following names were used for named storms that formed in the Northeastern Pacific Ocean during 1994. Names that were not assigned this season are marked in\n       <span style="color:gray;">\n        gray\n       </span>\n       . No names were\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_hurricane_names" title="List of retired Pacific hurricane names">\n        retired\n       </a>\n       , so this same list was used again in the\n       <a href="/wiki/2000_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2000 Pacific hurricane season">\n        2000 season\n       </a>\n       . This is the same list used for the\n       <a href="/wiki/1988_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="1988 Pacific hurricane season">\n        1988 season\n       </a>\n       except for\n       <i>\n        Ileana\n       </i>\n       , which replaced\n       <i>\n        Iva\n       </i>\n       and was used for the first time in 1994.\n      </p>\n      <table width="90%">\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Aletta\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Bud\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Carlotta\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Daniel\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emilia_(1994)" title="Hurricane Emilia (1994)">\n            Emilia\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Fabio\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilma_(1994)" title="Hurricane Gilma (1994)">\n            Gilma\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Hector\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Ileana\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a </li>\n          <li>\n           <div style="color: #888;">\n            Willa (unused)\n           </div>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <div style="color: #888;">\n            Xavier (unused)\n           </div>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <div style="color: #888;">\n            Yolanda (unused)\n           </div>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <div style="color: #888;">\n            Zeke (unused)\n           </div>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       For storms that form in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_Pacific_Hurricane_Center" title="Central Pacific Hurricane Center">\n        Central Pacific Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       \'s area of responsibility, encompassing the area between\n       <a href="/wiki/140th_meridian_west" title="140th meridian west">\n        140 degrees west\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">\n        International Date Line\n       </a>\n       , all names are used in a series of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_tropical_cyclone_names#Central_Pacific" title="List of tropical cyclone names">\n        four rotating lists\n       </a>\n       . The next four names that were slated for use in 1994 are shown below. Three of them,\n       <i>\n        Li\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <i>\n        Mele\n       </i>\n       , and\n       <i>\n        Nona\n       </i>\n       , were used throughout the course of the year.\n      </p>\n      <table style="width:90%;">\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Li\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Mele\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Nona\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span style="color:#666666">\n            Oliwa\n            <i>\n             (unused)\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Season_effects">\n        Season effects\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=1994_Pacific_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Season effects">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       This is a table of all the storms that have formed in the 1994 Pacific hurricane season. It includes their duration, names, landfall(s), denoted in parentheses, damages, and death totals. Deaths in parentheses are additional and indirect (an example of an indirect death would be a traffic accident), but were still related to that storm. Damage and deaths include totals while the storm was extratropical, a wave, or a low, and all the damage figures are in 1994 USD.\n      </p>\n      <table border="1" cellpadding="5" cellspacing="0"
